# Decision Log вЂ” Mission Control

Product, design and technical decisions for Mission Control (the Next.js app). Most recent on top. See the index and format in [DECISION-LOG.md](../../DECISION-LOG.md).

> The live project state is in [.pandacorp/status.yaml](../.pandacorp/status.yaml); the PRD in [docs/product/prd.md](product/prd.md) and the FRDs in [docs/frds/](frds/). This is where the **why** of the decisions goes, not the state.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Backlog reader: fail-loud on duplicate ids (FRD-22 AC-22-004.3, BL-0013)
**What:** `readBacklog()` now enforces id-uniqueness at the read boundary: two different `BL-*.md` files with the same `id` keep only the first in `items` and surface each collision in `errors[]` (`duplicate id BL-0010 (already defined in <file>)`), shown in the panel's fail-loud banner. Before, both files became items в†’ `BacklogPanel` rendered two children with the same React `key` в†’ a `console.error` that **intermittently red-locked the /proposals smoke gate** (caught only when the smoke test's error window overlapped a /proposals render).
**Why:** Root-caused while landing the promotions detail: the local `main` branch had two backlog files reusing ids BL-0010 and BL-0011 (a real data-integrity defect вЂ” exactly BL-0013's concern). The reader was clean in Node but the live factory data was not. Rather than depend on the data always being clean, MC now treats duplicate ids as the defect they are (DR-078 parse-don't-validate) and reports them instead of crashing the render. **Owner action still needed on the DATA:** renumber the two colliding files (`BL-0010-owner-activity-feed-вЂ¦`, `BL-0011-work-orders-lack-summary-вЂ¦`) to free ids (BL-0014/BL-0015) вЂ” MC now surfaces them in the banner instead of hiding them.
**Impact:** `src/lib/backlog/backlog.ts` (`readBacklog` dedup + fail-loud), `src/lib/backlog/_tests/backlog.test.ts` (duplicate-id case), `docs/frds/frd-22-factory-backlog/frd.md` (AC-22-004.3). Verified in-browser: the /proposals mobile render no longer emits the duplicate-key console error; the banner names both collisions. Bundled with the promotions-detail change at the owner's request (it was blocking that merge).

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Promotions queue: clean cards + click-to-open formatted detail (FRD-17, AC-17-006.7)
**What:** The promotions-queue cards no longer dump a raw 300-char markdown excerpt (which showed leaked `**Label:**`/`##` syntax and read as "code"). Each card now shows a **clean one-line summary** (the lesson's `context`, or the first body line with markdown markers stripped) as its title, plus the target chip, evidence and the copyable `/pandacorp:learn` command. The card's content is now a **clickable control** that opens the shared `LessonDetailModal` вЂ” the same sectioned, colour-coded detail the candidate/prune lessons and the backlog use вЂ” closing the follow-up deferred earlier today. The promotion detail additionally surfaces the `/pandacorp:learn` command (proposed only) so the owner can approve straight from the modal.
**Why:** Owner: the promotions card "sale sin formatoвЂ¦ las cositas de MarkdownвЂ¦ se ve feo"; wanted it pretty + click-to-open a formatted, ordered modal with all the info. The deferral reason (the queue lives in `components/modules/`, must not import route-local code) is resolved by the **callback split**: `PromotionsQueue` only emits `onSelectLesson`; a new route-local client wrapper `PromotionsQueuePanel` holds the modal state and renders `LessonDetailModal` вЂ” the exact pattern the candidate/prune streams use. Reuse over a new modal (DR-057/062): `LessonDetail`/`LessonDetailModal` gained one optional `command` prop rather than a forked promotion modal.
**Impact:** `components/modules/PromotionsQueue/PromotionsQueue.tsx` (now `"use client"`; optional `onSelectLesson`; clean `rationaleSummary`; clickable `EntryOpenRegion`; exported `buildLearnCommand` as the single source of the command); NEW `app/proposals/_components/PromotionsQueuePanel/` (+ `_tests/`); `LessonDetail.tsx` + `LessonDetailModal.tsx` (optional `command` в†’ copyable approve row); `app/proposals/page.tsx` (renders the panel); `docs/frds/frd-17-proposals-inbox/frd.md`. Tests: card shows the clean summary (no `**`); click calls `onSelectLesson`; the copy command is a sibling of the open button (no nested interactive); panel opens the modal with the sectioned body + approve command, rejected omits the command, Escape closes. The `PromotionsQueue` heading-role test was corrected to assert the real `SectionHead` label + region aria-label (the entries no longer carry an `<h3>`; `SectionHead` is deliberately a `<div>`, DR-062). Gate green.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Backlog detail = titled colour-coded sections; extracted the shared `SectionedMarkdown` primitive (FRD-22 / FRD-17)
**What:** The backlog item detail modal now renders its body as **titled, colour-coded sections** вЂ” the same treatment the memory-lesson detail got вЂ” instead of one plain `Markdown` block. Backlog bodies use `## Heading` sections (Problem / Root cause / Fix plan / Tests / Done when / Out of scope); each becomes a real section header (icon + coloured label + left accent rule) with its content as markdown. To avoid two parallel parsers, the sectioning logic (previously inline in `LessonDetail`) was **extracted into a shared `SectionedMarkdown` primitive** that auto-detects the section marker: `## Heading` mode when any line is an H2, else `**Label:**` mode. Both `LessonDetail` and `BacklogDetail` now consume it, so the two detail modals share exactly one look and one code path.
**Why:** Owner ask: "igual para el modal del backlog, hagamos que tenga un mejor formato, parecido a como hiciste con los de memoria." Extracting a shared primitive (rather than copy-pasting the lesson parser) satisfies reuse-before-create + visual coherence (DR-057, DR-062, DR-092) вЂ” the alternative was a second, drifting parser.
**Impact:** NEW `src/app/proposals/_components/SectionedMarkdown/SectionedMarkdown.tsx` (+ `_tests/`, covering both modes + the plain-body fallback); `LessonDetail.tsx` (inline parser removed в†’ consumes `SectionedMarkdown`); `BacklogPanel/BacklogDetail.tsx` (`Markdown` в†’ `SectionedMarkdown`); `docs/frds/frd-22-factory-backlog/frd.md` (AC-22-005.2) + `docs/frds/frd-17-proposals-inbox/frd.md`. Backlog detail test updated: `## Heading` sections now assert as section labels (via `within(body).getByText`), not `<h2>` headings. Gate green.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Memory-tab polish: card titles, colour-coded detail sections, correct command (FRD-17)
**What:** Four owner-reported fixes to the Memoria tab.
1. **Broken card titles fixed.** Cards derived their title from the body with a fragile heuristic that produced garbage (LESSON-0017 в†’ ".", LESSON-0018 в†’ "da"). Every lesson has a clean `context:` one-liner in its frontmatter; the memory reader now exposes `Lesson.context`, and the card uses it as the title. Removed the broken `deriveLessonTitle`/`LESSON_TITLE_MAX`.
2. **Detail body is now titled, colour-coded sections.** Lesson bodies use bold inline labels (`**Situation:**` / `**Lesson:**` / `**Apply next time:**` / `**Why it matters:**`); `LessonDetail` now parses those into distinct sections, each with an icon + coloured header (info/accent/ok/muted) + a left accent rule, content via `Markdown` вЂ” instead of one wall of bold-prefixed prose. (The parser is the flush-on-label pattern.)
3. **Group command corrected.** The candidate + prune lists' activating command was the bare `/pandacorp:memory`; it is now **`/pandacorp:memory review`** (the mode that corroborates/activates candidates and proposes pruning), matching the per-card command.
4. **"Obsoletas" explained in-UI.** Each stream now shows a one-line explainer under its title; the prune one says obsolete = `status: deprecated` (never-retrieved+old, or contradicted by newer evidence), set by review вЂ” never deleted.
**Why:** Owner: the memory cards looked broken (partial/garbage text), the command felt wrong, "obsoletas" was unexplained, and the detail was hard to read (bold text, no color). 
**Impact:** `src/lib/memory/memory.ts` (`Lesson.context`), `ProposalCard.tsx` (title from context; heuristic removed), `LessonDetail.tsx` (sectioned colour render), `page.tsx` (`MEMORY_GROUP_CMD` в†’ review), `streamMeta.ts` (prune description) + `DismissableProposalStream.tsx` (renders the per-stream explainer), `docs/frds/frd-17-proposals-inbox/frd.md`. ~15 test fixtures updated for the new required `context` field; tests for the sectioned render. Gate green.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Click a lesson card в†’ formatted detail modal (FRD-17, memory-tab parity with the backlog)
**What:** In Propuestas в†’ Memoria, clicking a **lesson** card (candidata / obsoleta) now opens a **detail modal** with the lesson's full, formatted body вЂ” same pattern as the backlog detail (FRD-22). New `LessonDetail` (metadata chips: typeВ·domain / status / eval-gate / promotion + source / links) + `LessonDetailModal` wrapper, reusing the shared `Modal` + `Markdown` primitives (DR-057, no reinvention). `ProposalCard`'s lesson card becomes an accessible `<button>` when given `onSelect` вЂ” but ONLY when it carries no per-card command (a CmdRow's CopyButton must not nest inside a button); the dismiss вњ• coexists as a sibling. `DismissableProposalStream` holds the selected-lesson state + renders the modal for lesson streams (candidate/prune); self-suggestions (no markdown body) stay non-clickable.
**Why:** Owner ask: "do the same [as the backlog detail] for the memory tab." The lesson's context (Situation / Lesson / Apply next time / Why it matters) lives in the body; the card only showed a derived title + chips.
**Impact:** NEW `src/app/proposals/_components/{LessonDetail,LessonDetailModal}.tsx`, `ProposalCard.tsx` (clickable lesson card + `onSelect`), `DismissableProposalStream.tsx` (selected state + modal), `docs/frds/frd-17-proposals-inbox/frd.md`. Tests: click opens the modal with the body as real headings; Escape closes; self-suggestions not clickable. Gate green. **Deferred (noted in the FRD):** the promotions-queue entries could gain the same detail, but it lives in `components/modules/` and importing a route-local detail there would cross the module boundary вЂ” a small follow-up (move the detail to `components/modules/` first).

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Click a backlog card в†’ formatted detail modal (FRD-22, REQ-22-005)
**What:** Clicking a card in Propuestas в†’ Backlog now opens a **detail modal** with the item's full, nicely-formatted content вЂ” the same look as the FRD/spec/doc detail elsewhere. Reused the existing primitives (no reinvention, DR-057): the shared `Modal` (focus-trap + Escape + backdrop-close) and the shared `Markdown` renderer. The backlog reader (`src/lib/backlog/backlog.ts`) now exposes each item's markdown **body** (`parsed.content`, previously discarded); a new `BacklogDetail` component renders the metadata chips (typeВ·area / severity / status + source / links / dates) above `Markdown(body)`, so the reformatted sections (Problem / Root cause / Fix plan / Tests / Done when) render as real headings/lists/code. `BacklogCard` became an accessible `<button>` (keyboard + aria-label) when given an `onSelect`; `BacklogPanel` became a client component holding the selected-item state + the modal.
**Why:** Owner ask: "clicking a backlog card should show a well-formatted detail, like the FRD detail on the board." The context (Problem/Fix plan/Tests) lives in the item body; without a detail view the card only showed the title + chips.
**Impact:** `src/lib/backlog/backlog.ts` (`BacklogItem.body`), NEW `src/app/proposals/_components/BacklogPanel/BacklogDetail.tsx`, `BacklogCard.tsx` (clickable button), `BacklogPanel.tsx` (в†’ client, modal), `docs/frds/frd-22-factory-backlog/frd.md` (REQ-22-005). Tests: modal open/close (Escape) + body rendered as headings. Reuses `core/Modal` + `core/Markdown` verbatim. Gate green.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” Limpieza del tab Memoria de Propuestas (FRD-17)
**What:** Paso 2 de la reorganizaciГіn de Propuestas (el Paso 1 fue el tab Backlog, FRD-22). Cuatro limpiezas al tab Memoria que el owner seГ±alГі como В«desordenadoВ»:
1. **Deduplicadas las promociones.** La pГЎgina mostraba las promociones DOS veces вЂ” un `DismissableProposalStream kind="promotion"` **y** la `PromotionsQueue`, ambos con el mismo dato. Se quitГі el stream redundante; queda solo la `PromotionsQueue` (REQ-17-006, la superficie rica: comando `/pandacorp:learn` + target + rationale + evidencia + badge de alto riesgo). Una promociГіn es un item В«apruГ©bameВ», no ruido para descartar.
2. **RediseГ±ado el botГіn В«DescartarВ».** De un pill con texto+borde colgando a la derecha de cada tarjeta (que el owner llamГі В«horribleВ») a un вњ• sutil, icon-only, en la esquina superior de la tarjeta (con `aria-label`, accesible por teclado).
3. **Borrado cГіdigo muerto.** `ProposalStream.tsx` (el stream no-dismissable, solo lo usaban los tests; la pГЎgina usa `DismissableProposalStream`). `streamMeta.ts` se moviГі a `_components/`; los tests de integraciГіn se reapuntaron a `DismissableProposalStream`.
4. **Filtradas las auto-sugerencias no ejecutables.** `unused-capability` emitГ­a `/pandacorp:<id>` para agentes tambiГ©n (no invocables como slash-command) в†’ ahora solo para **skills** invocables.
**Why:** El owner encontrГі la pГЎgina desordenada y confusa (dos secciones de promociones que parecГ­an lo mismo) y el botГіn de descartar feo. Estas cuatro limpiezas eran el hueco identificado en la auditorГ­a de la pГЎgina.
**Impact:** `src/app/proposals/page.tsx` (dedup), `src/app/proposals/_components/DismissableProposalStream/` (botГіn), `src/app/proposals/_components/streamMeta.ts` (movido) + `ProposalStream/` borrado, `src/lib/self-suggest/self-suggest.ts` (filtro), `docs/frds/frd-17-proposals-inbox/frd.md` (ACs actualizados). Tests actualizados a la estructura deduplicada. Gate verde. **Pendiente (deferido, distinto):** reconciliar el contador В«N abiertasВ» con los descartes (hoy los descartes son localStorage-only y el contador es server-side, asГ­ que puede sobrecontar) вЂ” es un refactor server/client aparte que merece su propio cambio.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” El backlog de la fГЎbrica se hace visible en Propuestas (FRD-22, DR-103)
**What:** La pГЎgina **Propuestas** ahora tiene dos sub-tabs вЂ” **Memoria** y **Backlog** вЂ” reusando la primitiva `Tabs`/`SubTabs` (DR-062, sin switcher a medida). El tab **Backlog** hace visible por primera vez la cola accionable de la fГЎbrica (`factory/backlog/BL-*`, el plano-3 de DR-103), que hasta ahora no se veГ­a en ningГєn lado y se perdГ­a. Componentes nuevos: `src/lib/backlog/backlog.ts` (reader **fail-loud** por DR-078 вЂ” un `BL-*` malformado se surface en `errors[]`, no desaparece; dir ausente = backlog legГ­timamente vacГ­o), `BacklogPanel` (agrupa por estado open/doing/done, nota read-only В«se trabajan pidiГ©ndoselo a un agenteВ», banner de error `role=alert`), `BacklogCard` (coherente con `ProposalCard`, DR-062), y `ProposalsTabs` (wrapper cliente; la pГЎgina Server Component lee ambos datasets y pasa cada panel como slot). El tab Memoria queda **idГ©ntico** (health + 4 streams + cola de promociones). MotivaciГіn del owner: В«si no hay visibilidad del backlog, se va a perderВ». Ambos tabs son "propuestas de modificaciГіn a la fГЎbrica", por eso comparten pГЎgina.
**Why:** DR-103 creГі `factory/backlog/` pero nada lo surfaceaba; sin visibilidad, los items (10 hoy) se olvidan. Los sub-tabs unifican memoria + backlog bajo un mismo concepto sin inventar navegaciГіn nueva.
**Impact:** NUEVO [FRD-22](frds/frd-22-factory-backlog/frd.md) (ACs REQ-22-001..004). NUEVO `src/lib/backlog/` (+ tests real/malformado), `src/app/proposals/_components/{BacklogPanel,ProposalsTabs}/` (+ tests). Editado `src/app/proposals/page.tsx` (lee el backlog, compone los tabs). Gate verde (tsc/biome/knip/vitest). **Pendiente (Paso 2, separado):** la limpieza del tab Memoria вЂ” deduplicar las dos superficies de promociones, rediseГ±ar el botГіn В«DescartarВ», reconciliar el contador con los descartes, borrar `ProposalStream.tsx` muerto, filtrar comandos no invocables en auto-sugerencias.

## 2026-07-01 вЂ” `vitest.config.ts` exclude fixed: no longer scans other worktrees' `node_modules`
**What:** `exclude` used bare `"node_modules"`, which only matches a literal top-level `node_modules` segment and did not stop vitest from recursing into `.claude/worktrees/<slug>/mission-control/node_modules/**` вЂ” the full checkouts of parallel manual sessions (DR-096) that live inside the main tree. `pnpm exec vitest run` picked up vendored test files there (e.g. `tsconfig-paths`'s own `__tests__/filesystem.test.ts`, which uses a deprecated Mocha-style `done()` callback Vitest 4 doesn't support) and reported ~1700 unrelated failures, redding `.pandacorp/verify.sh` for reasons that had nothing to do with this project's code. Fixed: `exclude` now uses `"**/node_modules/**"` (matches at any depth) plus an explicit `"**/.claude/worktrees/**"` entry.
**Why:** Surfaced while landing an unrelated worktree merge вЂ” the Stop gate failed on this project even though nothing in `src/` had changed. Root cause was config, not app code: the exclude pattern predates `.claude/worktrees/` holding full nested checkouts with their own `node_modules`.
**Verification:** `pnpm exec vitest run` went from 182 failed / 1154 passed test files to 383/383 passed (7360 tests, 2 expected fail) with no other change. Full `.pandacorp/verify.sh` re-run green end to end (unit + typecheck/lint/build + e2e).
**Impact:** `vitest.config.ts` only вЂ” no app behavior changed, no FRD affected.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Las 3 decisiones "colgadas" de `decisions.md` cerradas + `pending_decisions` a 0
**What:** El owner corriГі `/pandacorp:decide 2026-06-21-2` y el chequeo de vigencia (7+ dГ­as) confirmГі que las tres decisiones que todavГ­a parseaban como pendientes ya estaban resueltas hace dГ­as вЂ” solo que la resoluciГіn se habГ­a registrado como una entrada NUEVA arriba, dejando el bloque ORIGINAL sin tocar (por eso seguГ­an "pendientes" mecГЎnicamente). Verificado contra el estado real antes de cerrar: `WO-03-002` в†’ `VERIFIED` (OpciГіn A ya decidida arriba); `WO-06-006/011/013` (freeze de FRD-06) **ya ni existen** вЂ” FRD-06 se renumerГі/reconstruyГі por completo y estГЎ `VERIFIED`; `WO-06-004`/`WO-13-002` (regresiГіn de color) в†’ `VERIFIED`, ya resuelto en la entrada de arriba. Los tres bloques originales en `.pandacorp/inbox/decisions.md` (gitignored, sin commit) se editaron en el sitio: 2 в†’ `RESUELTO`, 1 в†’ `OBSOLETO`. `pending_decisions` en `status.yaml` corregido de `1` a `0` (cierra el "huГ©rfano" anotado en la entrada de abajo del mismo dГ­a).
**Why:** El owner notГі que el motor de build no parece limpiar estos registros cuando algo se decide en conversaciГіn o un agente lo resuelve solo вЂ” root cause confirmado y arreglado en el plugin (ver `plugin/docs/decision-log.md`, v9.38.1): ninguna skill documentaba editar el bloque ORIGINAL, asГ­ que la prГЎctica real era solo agregar una entrada narrativa nueva.
**Impact:** `content/manual/guides/g-feedback.md` (lГ­nea nueva sobre cerrar en el bloque original). `.pandacorp/inbox/decisions.md` y `.pandacorp/status.yaml` no se commitean (gitignored) вЂ” el estado real ya quedГі corregido en disco.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” `worktree-bootstrap.sh` fixed: `PANDACORP_FACTORY_ROOT` now actually exported for fresh worktrees
**What:** Closes the open item noted below (2026-06-30, "Hallazgo aparte"). `.pandacorp/worktree-bootstrap.sh` step 3 had a bare `:` no-op behind an MC-worktree detection condition, with a comment claiming the variable was exported elsewhere вЂ” it never was. `config.ts::resolveFactoryRoot()` falls back to `cwd/..` when `PANDACORP_FACTORY_ROOT` is unset, which in a fresh worktree resolves to that worktree's own empty `factory/` (gitignored files like `profile.md` aren't checked out), tripping `OnboardingGate.tsx` and reding every route in the e2e suite вЂ” not a cosmetic issue, the whole smoke gate goes red. Fixed: step 3 now writes a worktree-local, gitignored `mission-control/.env.local` with `PANDACORP_FACTORY_ROOT=$MAIN_WT`, the same pattern step 2 already uses for `launch.json`.
**Why:** Previously discovered and only worked around by hand (a throwaway `.env.local`, deleted before merge) вЂ” a footgun that had to be rediscovered and re-worked-around by whoever hit it next, the exact failure mode DR-096 (worktree self-isolation) exists to prevent.
**Verification:** Created a throwaway worktree, ran the fixed script, confirmed `mission-control/.env.local` was written and gitignored, and confirmed `resolveFactoryRoot()` now resolves to the main checkout (where `factory/profile.md` exists) instead of the worktree's empty copy.
**Impact:** `.pandacorp/worktree-bootstrap.sh` (this project's copy, synced directly), canonical source `plugin/templates/shared/.pandacorp/worktree-bootstrap.sh` + `plugin/templates/OVERLAY_VERSION` (8.52.0в†’8.52.1) + `plugin/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` (v9.38.2) вЂ” see `plugin/docs/decision-log.md`. `.pandacorp/status.yaml` `overlay_version` stays on its own pre-existing drift track (8.51.0в†’8.51.1, still behind the template вЂ” tracked separately as `mc-overlay-behind-template` in `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/`).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Los 8 hallazgos MC de la auditorГ­a de flujo в†’ cola de cambios del proyecto (DR-103)
**What:** La auditorГ­a de flujo de la fГЎbrica (`docs/proposals/19-factory-flow-audit-2026-06-30.md`, en panda-corp) tenГ­a varios hallazgos OPEN que son deriva especГ­fica de Mission Control. Por DR-103 (la memoria/backlog de la fГЎbrica es solo para la propia tooling de la fГЎbrica; la deriva de un proyecto va al inbox del proyecto) se rutean a la cola de cambios de MC. Se creГі `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/` (no existГ­a) con 8 change-cards `ready` + su `README.md` Г­ndice. ClasificaciГіn bug vs ajuste: **bug** в†’ `mc-verifysh-needs-clarification-gate` (gate de seguridad ausente), `mc-status-pending-counters-stale` (contadores que no reflejan realidad); **change/ajuste** (documentaciГіn/mantenimiento) в†’ los otros 6 (`mc-overlay-behind-template`, `mc-operation-vocabulary-sweep`, `mc-frd15-freshness-model-reconcile`, `mc-architecture-e2e-stale`, `mc-readonly-boundary-docs`, `mc-apimd-stale-regenerate`). Todas `class: standard` (ninguna rompe la app viva, 94/94 verde) con la prioridad de auditorГ­a (P0/P1/P2) anotada en el cuerpo. VerificaciГіn al vuelo (evidencia real, no snapshot): #1 real (overlay 8.51.0 vs plantilla 8.52.0), #2 y #5 **parecen ya resueltos** por sincronizaciones posteriores (el gate DR-100 ya estГЎ en `verify.sh` L47-59; `architecture.md` L310-316 ya documenta los 4 gates Playwright) в†’ marcadas "confirmar y cerrar, no reconstruir"; #4/#8 confirmados reales (`api.md` L1590-1668 sigue describiendo el contrato SHA como vigente). `pending_changes: 8` en `status.yaml` ya coincide y ahora estГЎ respaldado por archivos reales (antes era un contador huГ©rfano); `pending_decisions: 1` sigue huГ©rfano y se deja para que el owner confirme (no se autozerГі).
**Why:** SeparaciГіn de planos de DR-103: la deriva de un producto se traza en la cola del producto, no en `factory/backlog/`. Los hallazgos de tooling de la misma auditorГ­a ya viven en `factory/backlog/BL-0004..BL-0009`.
**Impact:** NUEVO `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/` (8 cards + `README.md`). Sin ediciГіn a mano de `status.yaml` (el contador ya era correcto; la regla dice que lo escriben skills/CI). El build drena estas `ready` en su prГіximo safe point (o el siguiente `/pandacorp:implement`).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” BotГіn "Aprobar la recomendaciГіn" eliminado; antigГјedad + estado OBSOLETO aГ±adidos
**What:** El owner pidiГі quitar el botГіn de un clic "Aprobar la recomendaciГіn" вЂ” sin el contexto completo de una conversaciГіn real con `/pandacorp:decide <id>`, aprobar a ciegas no tenГ­a sentido. Eliminado: `ApproveButton`, sus estilos, el import `CopyButton` ya sin uso. El texto de la recomendaciГіn se queda como contexto.
De paso, el owner preguntГі si `/pandacorp:decide` detecta decisiones obsoletas (decisiones de hace 1-2 semanas que el codebase probablemente ya superГі). No lo hacГ­a. Fix en dos capas:
1. **Mission Control:** `DecisionPoint` (`activity.ts`) gana `date: string | null` (la fecha del encabezado, para el indicador "hace N dГ­as") y `status: "pending" | "resolved" | "obsolete"` (antes `resolved` era binario; `SUPERSEDIDO`/`OBSOLETO` ahora son su propio estado, no se confunden con "resuelto"). `tab-summary.tsx` muestra el indicador de antigГјedad junto al id de cada tarjeta pendiente, y una etiqueta "Obsoleta" distinta para las tarjetas con `status: "obsolete"`.
2. **Plugin (`/pandacorp:decide`, v9.37.0):** chequeo activo de vigencia вЂ” si una decisiГіn tiene 7 dГ­as o mГЎs, el skill la marca y pregunta si sigue aplicando ANTES de pedir respuesta, leyendo el contexto real (el WO que bloquea, el cГіdigo referenciado) para opinar. Si el owner confirma que ya no aplica, el skill la registra como `OBSOLETO` (nunca `RESUELTO` вЂ” no se inventa una respuesta).
**Why:** Dos pedidos directos del owner en la misma conversaciГіn: (1) el botГіn de aprobar sin contexto era riesgoso, (2) faltaba una manera de descartar decisiones que el cГіdigo ya superГі sin tener que inventarles una respuesta.
**Impact:** `src/lib/docs/activity.ts`, `src/app/projects/[slug]/_components/tab-summary/tab-summary.tsx`, `docs/frds/frd-04-project-workspace/frd.md`, WO-04-001 + WO-04-005 (status notes). Contraparte en `plugin/skills/decide/SKILL.md` + `plugin/templates/docs/decisions-inbox-template.md` (commit aparte, mismo turno). 12 tests nuevos/actualizados.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Cada decisiГіn muestra su id y `/pandacorp:decide <id>` apunta solo a esa
**What:** El owner notГі que la tarjeta de decisiГіn solo decГ­a "corre `/pandacorp:decide`" sin indicar a cuГЎl tema se referГ­a вЂ” invocarlo en frГ­o recorre TODAS las pendientes una por una (confirmado en el skill). Fix: `DecisionPoint` (WO-04-001, `activity.ts`) gana un campo `id` derivado del propio encabezado (nunca inventado, nunca reutilizado) вЂ” `<YYYY-MM-DD>-<n>` para encabezados con fecha (`n` = posiciГіn 1-based entre los que comparten esa fecha exacta, contando pendientes Y resueltos, asГ­ el id nunca se mueve cuando un hermano cambia de estado), `legacy-<n>` para el formato `OPEN:/CLOSED:/RESOLVED:` sin fecha. WO-04-005 (`tab-summary.tsx`) ahora muestra el id en cada tarjeta (`data-testid="decision-id"`) y lo embebe en ambos comandos copiables: el genГ©rico (`/pandacorp:decide <id>`) y el de "Aprobar la recomendaciГіn" (`/pandacorp:decide <id> "Aprobado: вЂ¦"`).
**Contraparte en el plugin (mismo turno):** `/pandacorp:decide`'s SKILL.md fue enseГ±ado con la MISMA derivaciГіn de id + una regla de scoping (si el primer token de `$ARGUMENTS` matchea un id, salta directo a esa decisiГіn sin preguntar ni listar las demГЎs) вЂ” sin esto, el id mostrado en Mission Control serГ­a decorativo. Ver `plugin/docs/decision-log.md` (v9.36.0).
**Why:** Implementado directo (no vГ­a `/pandacorp:learn`+`skill-creator`) por ser una extensiГіn acotada y pedida explГ­citamente por el owner a un skill existente, no una capacidad nueva que justifique el pipeline completo de authoring+eval.
**Impact:** `src/lib/docs/activity.ts` (`DecisionPoint.id`, `_nextId`/`IdCounters`), `src/app/projects/[slug]/_components/tab-summary/tab-summary.tsx` (id visible + comandos embebidos), `docs/frds/frd-04-project-workspace/frd.md` (AC actualizado con el comando `<id>`-scoped), WO-04-001 + WO-04-005 (status notes), `content/manual/guides/g-feedback.md` (DR-046). 18 tests nuevos/actualizados (7 del esquema de id en `activity.ts`, exact-command tests del UI migrados al nuevo formato).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Party (La Fragua): el estado por-WO se reconcilia con el frontmatter autoritativo (forja vs Tribunal) вЂ” AC-06-001.6
**What:** La Party derivaba el estado de cada WO en ejecuciГіn **solo de los eventos** y lo fijaba a `building` a pelo (`fragua-snapshot.ts`), mientras la pestaГ±a Work Orders lee el estado **autoritativo** del frontmatter `implementation_status` (vГ­a `listWorkOrders`). Dos derivaciones independientes del mismo estado (el anti-patrГіn que DR-092 previene): el board mostraba `IN_REVIEW` y la Party seguГ­a mostrando el muГ±equito "construyГ©ndose" en la forja. Fix: `toFraguaSnapshot` acepta un mapa `woStates` (id в†’ `WoState`) y Гєsa esa como estado de cada WO en ejecuciГіn (fallback `building`); nuevo `toWoStates(listWorkOrders())` (`wo-states.ts`) mapea `reviewв†’in_review`, `doneв†’verified`, `failв†’blocked`, `todo/in_progressв†’building`. El motor (`engine.setWo`) ya camina el sprite a la sala correcta segГєn ese estado (forjaв†’Tribunalв†’BГіveda) вЂ” el Гєnico hueco era que el snapshot nunca le pasaba el estado real. El RSC (`ProjectWorkspace`в†’`PartyTab`) calcula `woStates` en cada render y lo **propaga al re-derive en vivo** (`PartyLiveShell`) para que un frame SSE (que solo lleva eventos) no revierta la sala a `building`. Guarda defensiva en `useFraguaSprites`: un WO `verified` en ejecuciГіn (que el motor ya convierte en trofeo vГ­a `setWo`) no se vuelve a sembrar desde `trophies` (evita doble conteo).
**Why:** El owner, viendo el `/implement` de personal-page-v2, notГі que WO-02-001 salГ­a "construyГ©ndose" en la Party pero `REVIEW/TESTING` en la pestaГ±a Work Orders, y pidiГі reconciliarlo con la fuente autoritativa (eligiГі "SГ­, reconciliar con frontmatter"). El frontmatter manda la sala; los eventos siguen dando la animaciГіn/liveness.
**Impact:** CГіdigo: `вЂ¦/_party/fragua-snapshot/fragua-snapshot.ts` (opt `woStates`), NUEVO `вЂ¦/_party/fragua-snapshot/wo-states.ts` (`toWoStates`), `вЂ¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyTab.tsx` + `PartyLiveShell.tsx` (prop `woStates` SSRв†’vivo), `вЂ¦/ProjectWorkspace.tsx` (cГЎlculo en el caso `party`), `вЂ¦/FraguaScene/useFraguaSprites.ts` (guarda dedup). Doc canГіnico: AC-06-001.6 (`docs/frds/frd-06-party/frd.md`). Tests: 6 en `wo-states.test.ts` + 6 en `fragua-snapshot.test.ts` (override in_review/blocked/verified, fallback, factory-off no resucita). **LГ­mite (documentado en el AC):** `woStates` se captura por render de la pestaГ±a (refresca al cambiar de tab / recargar); una transiciГіn con la pestaГ±a ya abierta se refleja en el siguiente render, no a mitad de frame вЂ” llevar `woStates` dentro del frame SSE queda como follow-up.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Party (La Fragua): un `wo` con el id del FRD ya no es un work order (avatar fantasma + contador inflado) вЂ” AC-06-001.5
**What:** El emisor de eventos escribe el campo `wo` con **el id del FRD** (`frd-02-home-positioning`) cuando la actividad es a nivel de FRD (un agente trabajando la feature como un todo, antes/entre sus work orders), no solo con ids reales (`WO-02-001`/`foundation`). `toFraguaSnapshot` trataba todo `wo` como un work order: aparecГ­a un **avatar fantasma** etiquetado con el id del FRD en la forja y el **contador global de WO se inflaba** (decГ­a `2` con un solo WO). Fix: helper `isFrdLevelWoId(wo)` (`/^frd-/i`) y se descarta el `wo` de nivel FRD en los tres procesadores de eventos (`processAgentWorking`, `processSubagentStop`, `processAchievement`) **y** en el conteo central `scan.allWoIds` dentro de `scanFrdData` вЂ” esta Гєltima era la **segunda fuente** que seguГ­a inflando el total aunque el sprite ya estuviera filtrado.
**Why:** El owner vio, con el `/implement` de personal-page-v2 corriendo, dos avatares (WO-02-001 correcto + uno "frd-02-home-positioning") y el contador en `2` existiendo un solo WO. DiagnosticГі con precisiГіn "la fuente viene de dos lados": efectivamente habГ­a dos sitios que aГ±adГ­an el `wo` al tally (los procesadores y el bucle central de `scanFrdData`); filtrar solo en los procesadores no bastaba.
**Impact:** CГіdigo: `src/app/projects/[slug]/_party/fragua-snapshot/fragua-snapshot.ts` (helper + 4 guardas). Doc canГіnico: AC-06-001.5 (`docs/frds/frd-06-party/frd.md`). Tests: 3 nuevos en `вЂ¦/_party/_tests/fragua-snapshot.test.ts` (un `wo`=id-de-FRD no entra en `running`, no infla `project.total`, ni cuenta como `done`/trophy). Pendiente aparte (NO en este cambio): la divergencia Party "building" vs pestaГ±a Work Orders "REVIEW" вЂ” es el problema de doble fuente de estado por-WO (eventos vs frontmatter `implementation_status`), a proponer al owner antes de tocarlo.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Decisiones pendientes: parser del formato real + fuente Гєnica para el badge (DR-092)
**What:** Dos defectos relacionados, encontrados por el owner al notar que el badge "1" del riel de portafolio no se correspondГ­a con nada visible en la secciГіn "Puntos de decisiГіn" del Resumen.
1. **Parser roto (`readDecisions`, WO-04-001).** Solo reconocГ­a encabezados `## OPEN:|CLOSED:|RESOLVED:` вЂ” un formato documentado pero que ningГєn `decisions.md` real usa. El formato real (el que `/pandacorp:decide` y los agentes escriben en la prГЎctica) es `## YYYY-MM-DD (<frase de estado>) вЂ” <tГ­tulo>`. La secciГіn "Puntos de decisiГіn" estaba estructuralmente vacГ­a siempre, sin importar el contenido del archivo. Fix: el parser ahora soporta ambos formatos (los 87 tests legacy siguen verdes sin tocar) + la lГ­nea machine-readable `- **Estado:**` de la plantilla como override cuando estГЎ presente. Nuevo export `countPendingDecisions(projectPath)` вЂ” el resolver Гєnico.
2. **Badge desincronizado (DR-092 вЂ” derivaciГіn duplicada).** El badge del riel (`ProjectRail`, WO-03-001) y el agregado "Tu turno" de Inicio (`guildState.ts`, WO-09-006) leГ­an `status.yaml: pending_decisions` вЂ” un contador de mantenimiento manual, distinto del que ya usaba correctamente el tab Resumen del proyecto (`readDecisions` directo). Ya habГ­an divergido: la Гєnica decisiГіn que generГі el `pending_decisions: 1` de Mission Control (WO-03-002, reusar `ProjectRail` vs el fork `SelectableProjectRail`) fue resuelta por el owner en conversaciГіn el 2026-06-21, pero nadie decrementГі el contador. Fix: nuevo wrapper `readStatusWithLiveDecisions` (WO-01-005) вЂ” `readStatus` + `pendingDecisions` sobreescrito con el conteo vivo; los dos call sites (`portfolio.ts::enrichEntry`, `guildState.ts::readGuildState`) ahora lo usan en vez de `readStatus` crudo.
**Why:** El owner notГі la inconsistencia probando la app; la causa raГ­z combinaba un parser que nunca matcheaba el formato real con dos derivaciones independientes del mismo contador (el patrГіn exacto que DR-092 existe para prevenir).
**Impact:** `src/lib/docs/activity.ts` (parser + `countPendingDecisions`), `src/lib/status/status.ts` (`readStatusWithLiveDecisions`), `src/lib/portfolio/portfolio.ts` + `src/lib/gamification/guildState.ts` (call sites). 16 tests nuevos. WOs: WO-04-001, WO-01-005, WO-03-001, WO-09-006 (status notes). No cambia ningГєn FRD/blueprint (el comportamiento documentado вЂ”"renderiza los puntos de decisiГіn, con badge de conteo"вЂ” no cambiГі, solo la fidelidad de la implementaciГіn al archivo real). `pending_decisions` en `status.yaml` queda como metadato sin tocar (otras skills lo escriben), pero deja de usarse como fuente para lo que ve el owner.
**Hallazgo aparte (infraestructura de worktrees, no corregido aquГ­):** el gate e2e de este worktree fallГі inicialmente en TODAS las rutas (no solo mobile) por un "onboarding gate" вЂ” `PANDACORP_FACTORY_ROOT` nunca se exporta de verdad para los worktrees de Mission Control; `.pandacorp/worktree-bootstrap.sh` В§3 tiene un placeholder no-op (`: # comment`) donde deberГ­a fijar la variable. Lo diagnostiquГ© y trabajГ© alrededor con un `.env.local` gitignored local al worktree para poder correr el gate вЂ” la correcciГіn real del script queda pendiente (no es parte de este bug).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” La Fragua: el martillo+brasa "forjando" reemplaza la barra de progreso indeterminada (AC-06-018.2)
**What:** SustituГ­ el indicador de la barra de progreso "trabajando" del sprite en la forja por un **martillo que golpea sobre la cabeza del muГ±equito + un halo de brasa cГЎlida** (`AgentSprite`). El martillo (рџ”Ё, `data-testid="agent-sprite-hammer"`, clase `fragua-hammer` con el keyframe `fragua-hammer-swing` de ~0.7s, `transform-origin` abajo-derecha para pivotar como un golpe) aparece SOLO en el estado `work`; el halo usa `--color-warn` (la brasa) en `work` y conserva `--color-cat-7` en `review`. EliminГ© por completo la barra: el bloque `agent-sprite-progress` (base/sweep indeterminados + el fill determinado), los estilos `progBarStyle`/`progFillStyle`, el local `isIndeterminate`, **y la prop `progress`** (ningГєn caller la pasaba). BorrГ© tambiГ©n las reglas CSS muertas `.fragua-bar-base`/`.fragua-bar-sweep`/`@keyframes fragua-bar-sweep`. El frame 0 del swing es una pose de reposo (martillo levantado, `rotate(-12deg)`) para que bajo `prefers-reduced-motion` quede un martillo estГЎtico levantado, no un fotograma a medio golpe.
**Why:** El owner eligiГі la opciГіn D del set propuesto: quiere que el sprite de la forja se sienta dinГЎmico/"forjando", pero **explГ­citamente NO una barra de progreso** вЂ” el progreso real ya lo transmite la sala/caminata entre habitaciones (AC-06-003.2/AC-06-013). El indicador es puro eye-candy, no un valor de progreso.
**Impact:** CГіdigo: `src/components/modules/party/AgentSprite/AgentSprite.tsx` (martillo + halo brasa, fuera barra y prop `progress`), `src/app/globals.css` (`fragua-hammer` + `@keyframes fragua-hammer-swing`; borradas las reglas `fragua-bar-*`). Doc canГіnico: AC-06-018.2 (`docs/frds/frd-06-party/frd.md`) reescrito de "barra indeterminada" a "martillo + brasa". Tests: `AgentSprite.test.tsx` y los adversariales `frd13-wo06-09.adversarial.reviewer.test.tsx` / `frd13-wo07-09.adversarial.reviewer2.test.tsx`. `bash .pandacorp/verify.sh` verde (380 test files, 7297 tests; tsc/biome/knip limpios; 66 e2e).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Observability timeline: cumulative FRDs + stale-state resolution
**What:** Fixed three defects in `readBuildTimeline()` (`src/lib/build-track/build-track.ts`):
1. FRDs built before `track.jsonl` was introduced (plugin v9.5.0) were invisible when TRACK mode was active вЂ” the function exclusively used track entries and ignored FRDs absent from the file. Fix: after `fromTrack()`, supplement with `fromStructural()` for every FRD not present in the track.
2. FRDs 9 and 10 appeared incomplete even though all their WOs were `VERIFIED` in frontmatter. Root cause: `wo_end state: "in_review"` was written to the track when the build was interrupted mid-reopen, leaving a stale intermediate state. `resolveWoState()` preferred this stale track state over the authoritative frontmatter. Fix: added `if (orderState === "done") return "done"` before the track end-state check.
3. WOs for a tracked FRD that had no track events were missing entirely. Fix: `supplementMissingWos()` adds them from the work-order list after the tracked WO loop.
Two helpers extracted (`groupOrdersByFrd`, `supplementMissingWos`) to keep `fromTrack()` under Biome's `noExcessiveCognitiveComplexity` cap (в‰¤15). Three new unit tests in group `(g)`.
**Why:** `track.jsonl` was introduced in plugin v9.5.0 (2026-06-23), after FRDs 1-8 were already built and verified. The TRACK mode silently excluded all pre-track FRDs, making the timeline look like only the last two FRDs existed. The stale-state issue made those FRDs appear in-progress despite being done. Together, the timeline was unreliable as a cumulative build history.
**Impact:** `src/lib/build-track/build-track.ts`, `src/lib/build-track/_tests/build-track.test.ts`. No FRD change needed (bug fix, no behavior-spec change). Mobile e2e failures in verify.sh are pre-existing in main (confirmed baseline; DR-099).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” FactoryWorktrees: secciГіn "ГЃrboles de trabajo" en Inicio (DR-096 В§7)
**What:** Nueva secciГіn `FactoryWorktrees` en la pantalla de Inicio que muestra los worktrees pendientes (sin mergear) de la fГЎbrica (panda-corp repo). PosiciГіn: entre Cartera y Progreso. Misma visual que TuTurno: SectionHead con chip de conteo/estatus + filas con tile de icono tintado por estado (stale=danger/`ti-clock-exclamation`, in-progress=accent/`ti-hammer`, ready=ok/`ti-git-merge`), nombre de rama, task label opcional, meta (estado В· commits В· horas) y comando de land copiable. Estados distintos para error vs vacГ­o (DR-078 fail-loud). Fuente de datos: `getPendingMerge()` вЂ” la misma funciГіn cacheada por request que ya usa el shell badge (DR-092, single source). No hay nueva fuente de datos ni nuevo API route. Nuevo archivo `src/components/dashboard/FactoryWorktrees/FactoryWorktrees.tsx` (Server Component) + tests en `_tests/` (14 tests, todos verdes).
**Why:** El mecanismo de enforcement de worktrees (DR-096/warn-adhoc-write.sh) impide dejar WIP, pero el discovery de worktrees olvidados era solo el shell badge (pequeГ±o, fГЎcil de ignorar) y la pestaГ±a de Summary por proyecto. La fГЎbrica necesita visibilidad propia porque sus worktrees NO son por proyecto вЂ” no aparecen en ninguna Summary tab. El owner pidiГі explГ­citamente una secciГіn en Inicio especГ­fica para worktrees de panda-corp.
**Impact:** `src/components/dashboard/FactoryWorktrees/FactoryWorktrees.tsx` (nuevo componente), `src/components/dashboard/FactoryWorktrees/_tests/FactoryWorktrees.test.tsx` (14 tests), `src/app/page.tsx` (import + call `getPendingMerge()` + render secciГіn 5b). No hay nueva fuente de datos; no hay cambio de overlay ni de standards; no hay FRD nuevo (es una adiciГіn al FRD-18 existente del dashboard Inicio). Registrado en decision-log Гєnicamente.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Party (La Fragua): WO sprites now WALK between rooms (AC-06-003.2 IMPLEMENTED)
**What:** The La Fragua engine already computed the walk вЂ” `engine.tick(now)` interpolates each sprite's `px,py` toward its target room slot (forgeв†’tribunalв†’vault), and `engine.wos()` returns the current animated positions in stage coordinates вЂ” but `FraguaScene` ran the RAF loop calling `engine.tick()` and **never read the output**: running WO sprites were placed STATICALLY at fixed room slots (`FORGE_SLOTS[idx]` inside `<Room zone="forge">`, in-review sprites at `REVIEW_SLOTS` inside the tribunal). So a WO **jumped** between rooms on a state change instead of walking. Fix: render the moving WO sprites as a single **stage-level layer** (one wrapper per `snapshot.running`, NOT split by room, directly under `fragua-stage`), each holding a stable ref in a `Map<wo, HTMLDivElement>`; the RAF loop now reads `engine.wos()` after each `engine.tick(performance.now())` and writes `el.style.left/top` **imperatively** (no `setState` per frame). React owns the sprite LIST; the RAF loop owns their POSITIONS. The forge/tribunal `Room`s stay as background layers; the vault TROPHY sprites stay static. First paint uses the static forge-slot fallback for SSR stability, then the effect/RAF takes over. Under `prefers-reduced-motion` a single paint places each sprite in the correct room with no RAF loop. Extracted into `useFraguaSprites.ts`.
**Why:** The walk animation was specified (AC-06-003.2) and fully computed by the engine, but dead вЂ” the scene never consumed `engine.wos()`. Figures teleporting between rooms is exactly the "figure stranded mid-path" the AC forbids.
**Impact:** Code: `вЂ¦/_party/FraguaScene/FraguaScene.tsx` (stage-level sprite layer + hook wiring; removed in-room running/in-review maps + the now-unused `REVIEW_SLOTS`), NEW `вЂ¦/_party/FraguaScene/useFraguaSprites.ts`. Docs: `frd-06-party/frd.md` (AC-06-003.2 IMPLEMENTED). Tests: NEW `вЂ¦/FraguaScene/_tests/FraguaScene.walk.test.tsx` (controlled RAF + mocked `performance.now`); updated `FraguaScene.test.tsx`. Gate fully green (vitest 7298 + tsc/biome/knip + 66 e2e). Caveat: the walk is only **visually** observable with a live build emitting state-flipping events; verified deterministically by the engineв†’DOM unit test.

No production `src/` change. **Validated by running `bash .pandacorp/canary.sh` here: 8/8 gates rejected their broken input, exit 0, sandbox cleaned** вЂ” plus a negative test confirming it flags a rotted (green) gate.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Party factory-off survives the SSE replay (PartyLiveShell, AC-06-013.4 follow-up)
**What:** Follow-up to the same-day factory-off fix. The server (`PartyTab`) correctly rendered the powered-off scene from `status.yaml running:false`, but AFTER hydration the scene re-activated: `PartyLiveShell` re-derives the snapshot from each SSE frame via `toFraguaSnapshot`, and `/api/live` emits the current event tail on connect even when the build is OFF в†’ `liveFrame` becomes non-null with the STALE tail в†’ the re-derive ran WITHOUT `running` в†’ `active:true` again (phantom WO + lit beat returned). Fix: thread `running` into `PartyLiveShell`; in the re-derive, a frame whose `lastEventAt` is NOT newer than the page-load snapshot is treated as a mere replay and keeps `running:false` (powered-off); a genuinely newer event (ISO-8601 `>`) reactivates (the build resumed, AC-06-013.3). `PartyTab` passes `running` to `PartyLiveShell`.
**Why:** Verified on `:1987` after the first fix: SSR HTML showed 0 running sprites (off, correct) but the hydrated client showed `runningSprites:1` + `litBeats:2` вЂ” the SSE replay undid the server's factory-off. The initial fix only covered the RSC snapshot, not the live re-derive. Caught by a browser check, not the unit gate (the unit test exercised the pure snapshot, not the SSE path). Added a `PartyLiveShell` test that mocks `useLiveSnapshot` with a stale replay vs a fresher event.
**Impact:** Code: `вЂ¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyLiveShell.tsx` (+`running` prop, replay-vs-fresher logic), `вЂ¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyTab.tsx` (pass `running`). Tests: `PartyLiveShell.factoryoff.test.tsx` (NEW). Same AC-06-013.4 contract; no new doc surface.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Manual (CГіdice del gremio) actualizado: rename architecture + digest + pestaГ±a Arquitectura (DR-046)
**What:** Sincronizado el Manual con los cambios de esta tanda (DR-046: el Manual refleja la superficie operable). ## 2026-06-30 вЂ” DAG de dependencias por-FRD dentro del modal de cada FRD (Arquitectura tab, AC-02-013.6)
**What:** En el tab Arquitectura, al abrir el modal de un FRD, ahora se muestra al final un **DAG acotado a
ese FRD** вЂ”reutilizando el mismo `WoDag` del Plan de implementaciГіnвЂ” con solo las work orders de ese FRD y
sus dependencias/paralelismo intra-FRD. Solo aparece cuando el FRD tiene **mГЎs de una** work order (con una
sola no hay nada que graficar, asГ­ que se omite). Las WOs por FRD se cruzan con las live `workOrders`
(`listWorkOrders`) por nГєmero de FRD (`workOrdersForFrd` + `frdKey`: "FRD-01" в†” "frd-01-вЂ¦"); el DAG dropea
las deps cross-FRD (esos nodos no estГЎn en el subconjunto), mostrando la cadena interna del FRD.
**Why:** Pedido del dueГ±o: ver dependencias y paralelismo de cada FRD sin tener que escanear el DAG global;
y que no aparezca para FRDs de una sola WO. Reutiliza el componente existente (cero librerГ­a nueva, DR-062).
**Context:** Verificado contra `personal-page-v2`: FRD-01 (4 WOs) muestra el DAG con su cadena
WO-01-001в†’вЂ¦; los FRDs de 1 WO (Home, Contact, вЂ¦) no lo muestran. Tests: `ArchitectureDigest.test.tsx`
(gating >1 vs 1 WO, DAG acotado a las WOs del FRD).
**Impact:** CГіdigo: `src/app/board/_components/CardDetail/ArchitectureDigest/ArchitectureDigest.tsx`
(`workOrdersForFrd`/`frdKey` + `FrdModal` con DAG condicional). Doc canГіnico: `frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md`
(AC-02-013.6). Extiende REQ-02-013. Sin cambio de plugin (solo MC).

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Party: factory-off from `status.yaml running` (AC-06-013.4) + bridges below the rooms
**What:** Two Party (La Fragua) bug fixes. **(1) Factory-off detection.** `toFraguaSnapshot` set `active: true` whenever the event tail had a FRD вЂ” with NO freshness/running check. The `~/.claude/dashboard-events.ndjson` keeps the LAST build's events forever, so after a build finished the scene stayed "active": a frozen lit "Oleada" beat + a phantom running WO (the final Visual-QA pass). Fix: thread the project's authoritative `running` flag (already read in `ProjectWorkspace` from `status.yaml`) в†’ `PartyTab` в†’ `toFraguaSnapshot`; when `running === false` the snapshot is forced to the powered-off state (`active:false`, `running:[]`, gate closed). `PartyTab` now gates scene-vs-empty on **`frd !== null`** (a build EXISTS) instead of `active`, so an OFF build still renders the scene's grey powered-off design (the `PowerOffOverlay`, AC-06-013) rather than the never-built empty state; and `PartyScene` lights NO flow-strip beat when off (`activeKeys = active ? вЂ¦ : []`). The SSE re-derive (`PartyLiveShell`) deliberately does NOT receive `running` вЂ” a live event frame means the build IS active, so a stale page-load `running` must not suppress a build that just started. Known nuance: a build that stops WHILE the tab is open updates on the next RSC render (reload/nav), not instantly вЂ” acceptable per AC-06-013.3 (events resume в†’ active). **(2) Stone bridges z-order.** The bridges' endpoints overlap the room rectangles (coords 415вЂ“505 over forge 16вЂ“448 + tribunal 472+), and at the prototype's `z-index:2` they sat visibly ON TOP of the room art. Owner-requested: bridges BELOW the rooms. Lowered `StoneBridge` root `z-index` 2в†’0 (above only the stage grid; rooms are z-index 1, sprites z-index 5) and updated the prototype `la-fragua.html .bridge` to match.
**Why:** Owner testing on `:3000`/main with the factory OFF: "se quedГі congeladoвЂ¦ aparece un work order Visual QA que no deberГ­aвЂ¦ si la fГЎbrica estГЎ apagada deberГ­amos mostrar el diseГ±o de fГЎbrica apagada"; and "los puentes deberГ­an aparecer abajo de las imГЎgenes de las salas, ahorita aparecen encima". Root cause of (1): event-presence в‰  build-running; only `status.yaml running` distinguishes them. Found while testing (bugs), fixed directly in an isolated worktree (DR-096) with TDD.
**Impact:** Code: `вЂ¦/_party/fragua-snapshot/fragua-snapshot.ts` (`running` opt в†’ factory-off), `вЂ¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyTab.tsx` (`running` prop + `frd`-gated body), `вЂ¦/projects/[slug]/ProjectWorkspace.tsx` (pass `running`), `вЂ¦/_party/PartyScene/PartyScene.tsx` (no lit beats when off), `components/modules/party/StoneBridge/StoneBridge.tsx` (z-index 0). Docs: `frd-06-party/frd.md` (AC-06-013.4), `frd-06-party/mocks/la-fragua.html` (`.bridge` z-index). Tests: `fragua-snapshot.factoryoff.test.ts` (NEW), `StoneBridge.test.tsx` (+z-index). No Party visual baseline exists, so the z-order change trips no visual gate.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Eliminado `docs/proposals/` en MC; regla reforzada en fГЎbrica y proyecto
**What:** Deleted `mission-control/docs/proposals/architecture-tab-and-skill-rename.md` (stale context doc вЂ” the work was already shipped in commit `56e31f7`). Removed the empty `docs/proposals/` folder. Added an explicit "Forbidden pattern" prohibition to `factory/standards/documentation.md` and to `docs/rules/documentation-and-decisions.md`: a project **never** has `docs/proposals/`; pending changes always go to `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/` via `/pandacorp:change`.
**Why:** An agent created the folder as a "context doc for an implementation session" instead of using the change inbox. The file was invisible to the build engine and Mission Control's queue, so it would never have been automatically picked up. The rule needed to be written explicitly because the documentation standard listed what *was* allowed but never said what was forbidden.
**Impact:** `factory/standards/documentation.md` (new "Forbidden pattern" section); `docs/rules/documentation-and-decisions.md` (same); deleted `docs/proposals/` folder.

## 2026-06-30 вЂ” Factory-flow audit: overlay upgrade + doc-drift reconciliation (operationв†’release, FRD-15 semver, Playwright)
**What:** Applied the Mission-Control findings of the factory-flow audit (`docs/proposals/19-factory-flow-audit-2026-06-30.md`):
- **Overlay upgraded 8.44.0 в†’ 8.48.0 + DR-100 gate installed (P0-1/P0-2).** `.pandacorp/verify.sh` was behind the canonical Next.js template and **missed the DR-100 residual-ambiguity gate** (a `[NEEDS CLARIFICATION]` marker in an `status: ACTIVE` doc must RED). Synced `verify.sh` verbatim to the template (adds the DR-100 block) and re-synced the other managed overlay scripts (`pending-work.sh`, `merge-queue.sh` вЂ” now carrying the audit's JSON-escaping + busy-main preflight hardening). Verified MC carries no `[NEEDS CLARIFICATION]` in an ACTIVE doc, so the new gate doesn't red-lock the build. Bumped `overlay_version` to 8.48.0 and the `guide.md` pipeline line off the obsolete `operation` phase.
- **`operation` phase swept from FRD docs + prototype (P0-3).** DR-085 had folded `operation` into `release` in the code (the `Phase` type is `product|design|architecture|implementation|release`; active set `architecture|implementation|release`; `release`в†’shipped column), but FRD-01/02/03/04/09 docs and `docs/design/prototype/index.html` still listed `operation` as a live phase/Phase-union value/active-set member/command key. Corrected all current-state assertions to match the code; preserved the "DR-085: operation folded into release" history. (Files: frd-01 blueprint + wo-01-005; frd-02 frd/fdd/blueprint + wo-02-001/003/011; frd-03 blueprint + wo-03-001; frd-04 blueprint + wo-04-003; frd-09 wo-09-001; prototype index.html.)
- **FRD-15 reconciled to the semver model (P0-4).** `frd.md` was already amended (2026-06-22) to compare installed vs source plugin **semver `version`** (the signal `claude plugin update` uses), but the `blueprint.md` and `work-orders/` still described the abandoned git-commit-SHA + dirty-state model (frozen installed SHA в†’ permanent false "behind" alarm). Rewrote them to the semver contract (`readInstalledVersion`/`readPluginSourceVersion`/`getPluginSyncState`, reasons behind/in-sync/unknown, banner only on "behind", null-on-unreadable); retired REQ-15-001/REQ-15-003; SHA model kept only as labelled history.
- **Architecture + PRD reconciled (P1-1/P1-12).** `docs/product/architecture.md` now reflects the real fail-closed gate chain and the four Playwright browser gates (smoke DR-055, visual DR-056, responsive DR-074, shell DR-075) instead of "no Playwright/e2e in v1"; the phase enum dropped `operation`; plugin-sync described as semver, not SHA. The bounded-write set (discard/restore `status` ADR-0002, visual `favorite` ADR-0003) is now stated consistently in architecture and PRD (the PRD no longer frames discard as the only write).
- **`docs/api.md` reconciled (P2).** Hand-maintained (no generator found). Removed `operation` as a live phase everywhere (Phase union, `workspaceCommands`, `activeProjects`, `deriveColumn`, `nextStep`, FRD-12 KPI) and replaced the plugin-sync SHA description with the semver contract; fixed two latent current-state errors surfaced during the sweep (`deriveColumn` `release`в†’shipped, `nextStep` `release`в†’`/pandacorp:iterate`), verified against the live `lib/` modules.
- **Pending-queue items classified (P1-10).** `phase: release` with `pending_decisions: 1` + `pending_changes: 8` is **not** unfinished work hiding behind green: `pending_changes` = 5 `ready` + 3 `draft` post-release backlog (already classified in the gitignored `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/README.md`); `pending_decisions: 1` is WO-03-002 (owner resolved it Option A; the action is in-flight). Surfacing these in the MC UI is already captured as the backlog item `mc-pending-items-view.md`. No counters were touched (an active parallel session owns the WO-03-002 work вЂ” DR-099).
**Why:** P0вЂ“P2 documentation-drift findings вЂ” canonical docs that name a phase the code no longer has, or a plugin-sync model the code abandoned, mislead any agent/skill reading them and break the FRDв†”code traceability spine; the overlay was behind the current gate standard.
**Impact:** `.pandacorp/{verify.sh,pending-work.sh,merge-queue.sh,status.yaml,guide.md}`; `docs/product/{architecture.md,prd.md}`; `docs/api.md`; FRD-01/02/03/04/09 docs + work-orders; FRD-15 blueprint + work-orders; `docs/design/prototype/index.html`. ## 2026-06-29 вЂ” Fix: el deep-link `/projects/[slug]` daba 404 para TODOS los proyectos
**What:** La pГЎgina de workspace resolvГ­a el proyecto con `activeProjects().find((p) => p.name === slug)` вЂ”
contra el nombre CRUDO ("Pandacorp (Mission Control)")вЂ”, pero el dashboard/portafolio (Cartera) generan el
href con un slug **kebab** (`nameToSlug` в†’ "pandacorp-mission-control"). Nunca coincidГ­an в†’ **404 en todo el
workspace de proyecto** (Party, Observabilidad, Documentos, etc.). Se extrajo `nameToSlug` a un helper
compartido (`src/lib/slug.ts`, un solo origen вЂ” DR-092) y la pГЎgina ahora resuelve por slug
(`nameToSlug(p.name) === slug`), tolerando ademГЎs el nombre crudo para enlaces directos antiguos.
**Why:** Bug descubierto al intentar mostrar el Party: el deep-link estaba roto en main (el dueГ±o veГ­a una
pestaГ±a vieja en cachГ©; un refresh daba 404). El generador de enlaces y el resolutor deben compartir la
MISMA transformaciГіn nombreв†’slug o todo deep-link 404ea. Hueco de cobertura: el Preview Smoke Gate cubre
`/board`, `/portfolio`, `/achievements`, `/manual` pero **no** `/projects/[slug]` con un slug real, por eso
pasГі todos los gates estГЎticos con la pantalla en 404.
**Context:** Test unitario de `nameToSlug` (incluye el caso exacto que rompГ­a). Fix de correctitud, separado
de la animaciГіn del Party (REQ-06-018). Pendiente sugerido: aГ±adir el deep-link de proyecto al smoke gate.
**Impact:** CГіdigo: `src/lib/slug.ts` (NUEVO), `src/app/projects/[slug]/page.tsx`. Tests: `src/lib/_tests/slug.test.ts` (NUEVO).

## 2026-06-29 вЂ” Party (La Fragua): liveness continua вЂ” la escena se ve VIVA entre eventos (REQ-06-018)
**What:** Nueva REQ-06-018 + implementaciГіn. El Party se veГ­a **estГЎtico/muerto** durante builds reales: se
alimenta solo del stream de eventos de Claude Code y solo se movГ­a en las *transiciones* entre eventos, asГ­ que
con un agente moliendo una sola WO ~9 min sin eventos el muГ±equito llegaba a su hueco y se congelaba. DiagnГіstico
a nivel de cГіdigo: los sprites se renderizan estГЎticos desde el snapshot en posiciones fijas y el motor RAF
(`engine.tick`) se ejecutaba pero **su salida nunca se volcaba al DOM** в†’ nada animaba; ademГЎs el "halo pulsante"
del contrato de diseГ±o de `AgentSprite` **nunca se implementГі** (solo opacidad fija) y la barra recibГ­a `progress=0`
sin fuente. Se aГ±adiГі **animaciГіn ambiente continua por CSS** (no dependiente de eventos): bob + halo pulsante en
sprites en estado `work`/`review` (reusa el keyframe `campaign-idle-bob`), barra **indeterminada honesta** (sweep,
sin inventar %), **latido global "forjando en vivo / sin seГ±al reciente / en espera"** derivado de `active` +
frescura real de `lastEventAt` (umbral 4 min), y un **pulso suave en el beat activo** de la FlowStrip. Todo se
auto-desactiva con `prefers-reduced-motion` (regla global de `globals.css`) cayendo a un estado estГЎtico visible
(coherente con AC-06-014.1). **No** se inventa progreso ni datos (DR-078/087): la barra indeterminada es una seГ±al
de actividad, no un porcentaje.
**Why:** El dueГ±o reportГі (dos veces, mirando `:1987`) que "no se mueve nada, se ve sГєper estГЎtico": muГ±equitos
quietos, barra que nunca sube, y un sprite que aparecГ­a/desaparecГ­a. La causa raГ­z es de diseГ±o (visualizaciГіn
100% event-driven sin seГ±al de vida ambiente) + dos defectos (halo no implementado, barra sin fuente). Una vista
de "vida" no puede depender solo de eventos discretos. Construido directo (el dueГ±o eligiГі "arreglarlo ya"),
aislado en worktree para no chocar con el build de FRD-09/10 en curso (DR-096).
**Context:** TDD вЂ” tests de las clases de animaciГіn (AgentSprite, FlowStrip), `deriveHeartbeat` como funciГіn pura,
y la transiciГіn vivoв†’stale con fake timers; se actualizГі el test adversarial `frd13-wo07-09.reviewer2` que
codificaba el comportamiento viejo (progress=0 в†’ fill 0%) al nuevo (indeterminado). Gate completo verde
(vitest 7147 + tsc/knip/biome + e2e/visual 56). Queda **pendiente** (capturado en la change-card
`mc-party-liveness-heartbeat.md`): arreglar de raГ­z el **parpadeo** aparecer/desaparecer (la presencia del sprite
debe gobernarla `wo_start`/`wo_end` de `.pandacorp/track.jsonl`, no `AgentWorking`/`SubagentStop`) y leer el pulso
real del build вЂ” es un cambio de la derivaciГіn (`fragua-snapshot.ts`) con mayor radio de tests, separado de este.
**Impact:** CГіdigo: `src/app/globals.css` (keyframes + clases liveness), `components/modules/party/AgentSprite/AgentSprite.tsx`,
`components/modules/party/FlowStrip/FlowStrip.tsx`, `app/projects/[slug]/_party/PartyScene/PartyScene.tsx` (+ `deriveHeartbeat`).
Docs: `docs/frds/frd-06-party/frd.md` (REQ-06-018). Tests: AgentSprite, FlowStrip, PartyScene.heartbeat (nuevo),
frd13-wo07-09.reviewer2 (actualizado). Sin tocar el motor de derivaciГіn (parpadeo/pulso real = follow-up).

## 2026-06-29 вЂ” WO-09-006: gamification ledger вЂ” persistent XP accumulator
**What:** Implemented the gamification ledger (`factory/gamification-ledger.json`, gitignored) that
records the historical maximum guild outcomes (workOrdersDone, phasesCompleted, releases) so that
deleting a project NEVER decreases the guild's XP or level. Three new artifacts: (1)
`lib/gamification/ledger.ts` вЂ” pure module with `readLedger` (DR-078 compliant: never throws,
zero-totals on absent/malformed), `mergeLedgerOutcomes` (MAX(live, ledger) per metric), and
`needsSnapshot` (detects when a write is needed); (2) `app/_actions/snapshotLedger.ts` вЂ” Server
Action that reads, compares, and writes the ledger only when needsSnapshot is true (fire-and-forget,
never blocks render); (3) `GamificationLedgerSync` client component (renders null) mounted in
`app/page.tsx` вЂ” calls the action once after hydration. Integration: the ledger merge now happens
inside `readGuildState()` in `lib/gamification/guildState.ts` (the single source of truth) so all
three surfaces (GuildBar, dashboard, Logros hero) pick up the ledger floor at once. `GuildState`
exposes both `liveOutcomes` (pre-merge, for the snapshot action) and `outcomes` (post-merge, for the
level computation). `factory/gamification-ledger.json` added to the factory root `.gitignore`.
**Why:** AC-09-006.1вЂ“3 (FRD-09). Ensures historical XP is never lost when a project is deleted.
The write is fire-and-forget (never blocks TTFB). Personal data вЂ” gitignored (DR-033).
**Impact:** `docs/frds/frd-09-gamification/frd.md` (AC-09-006 already present); `docs/design/components.md`
(new `GamificationLedgerSync` row); `.gitignore` (ledger entry); `lib/gamification/guildState.ts`
(ledger merge integrated into single source of truth).

## 2026-06-29 вЂ” FRD-10 v3: el tab EstadГ­sticas pasa a "Informe operativo" (spec + work orders)
**What:** IteraciГіn aprobada del SalГіn de Logros (FRD-10): el tab **EstadГ­sticas** se expande de la hoja
de personaje (radar + rГ©cords + ledger) a un **Informe** sobrio para el operador, alimentado solo por
datos REALES. Spec aГ±adida (aditiva, no borra criterios): nueva sub-feature **"Informe operativo"** en el
`frd.md` con REQ-10-020..027 y AC-10-020.K..027.K en EARS вЂ” seis bandas (1) **El pulso de la fГЎbrica**
(veredicto por reglas + KPIs de flujo: WO verificados/sem + delta, WIP, conversiГіn ideaв†’launched, y
**lead time ideaв†’release marcado "no cableado"** porque `readIdeas` aГєn no parsea `created`), (2) **En el
tiempo, de verdad** (WO-verificados-por-semana desde el historial git de cada `wo-*.md` al cruzar a
`VERIFIED` + ideas-por-semana desde `created`; **reemplaza** la vista de conteo crudo de eventos = ruido),
(3) **CГіmo usas la fГЎbrica** (workflows + mezcla de esfuerzo desde el event stream), (4) **Embudo y
flujo** (funnel ideasв†’launched + transiciones de fase **por proyecto** desde el historial git de cada
`status.yaml`, con flag de **reapertura** texto+icono), (5) **Estado y salud del proceso** (2 columnas:
proyectos por fase + seГ±ales del proceso: lecciones 2/131, relanzamientos, descartes sin razГіn
estructurada, telemetrГ­a de calidad "no cableado"), (6) **QuГ© mover ahora** (next-actions con su comando).
AdemГЎs: ledger a **8 filas por columna** (alineado, sin escalera; ProducciГіn += FRDs/Commits/Proyectos,
Calidad += Tests/DR) y rГ©cords a **grid 2Г—3** (+ Peak week, Lessons captured, Subagents). Se crearon dos
work orders **coarse**: **WO-10-014** (capa de datos: `IF-10-flow-series`/`IF-10-phase-transitions`/
`IF-10-scalars`/`IF-10-usage`/`IF-10-funnel`/`IF-10-lessons` + reglas veredicto/next-action; fail-loud,
git en lectura) y **WO-10-015** (UI de las 6 bandas + ledger 8 filas + rГ©cords 2Г—3, dependsOn WO-10-014).
Ancla visual aprobada: `docs/design/prototype/informe-del-gremio.html`.
**Why:** El dueГ±o aprobГі el diseГ±o del Informe (registro sobrio, DR-062 вЂ” la lore/niveles se quedan en
Trofeos/Rangos). El contrato de honestidad se mantiene (DR-078: cualquier cifra sin fuente cableada se
pinta **"вЂ”"/"no cableado"**, nunca un cero fabricado; los readers fallan en voz alta; **only-grow NO
aplica a la serie temporal** вЂ” una semana puede bajar). Los nГєmeros esperados de cada AC vienen de datos
verificados de la fГЎbrica (W25=78/W26=8/W27=5; ideas 18в†’1в‰€6%; workflows deep-research 1494 / build 850;
esfuerzo high 1384/xhigh 937/max 700/medium 3; FRDs 21 / commits 823 / tests 7134 / DR 99; lecciones
2/131; transiciones de mission-control incl. la reapertura del 06-19), no inventados.
**Context:** Solo spec/markdown вЂ” no toca el gate (`tsc`/`knip`/visual no leen `docs/`). Las nuevas WO van
**PLANNED**; el patrГіn de lectura git fail-soft se reutiliza de `lib/build-track.ts` (`readGitLog` via
`execSync`, pathspec acotado + `-n`, cache por request) con el caveat de rendimiento anotado en el
blueprint. El `frd.md` queda con un `[NEEDS CLARIFICATION]` cero вЂ” el Гєnico hueco real (lead time ideaв†’
release) estГЎ resuelto como decisiГіn: ship "no cableado" hasta que exista el emisor (`docs/achievements.md`
В§8 pending-emitter). Cascada de docs completa: FRD (sub-feature + frontmatter `visual_source_informe`),
blueprint (В§3 readers v3 + В§4 `CMP-10-informe` + Build Plan), FDD (banda EstadГ­sticas в†’ Informe),
work-orders/README (secciГіn v3 + tabla).
**Impact:** Docs: `docs/frds/frd-10-achievements-hall/{frd.md, blueprint.md, fdd.md, work-orders/README.md,
work-orders/wo-10-014-informe-data-layer.md (NUEVO), work-orders/wo-10-015-informe-ui.md (NUEVO)}`. Sin

**Why:** El dueГ±o pidiГі actualizar "toda la documentaciГіn (FRD, blueprints, work orders, FDD)" tras
