A third role-color touch-point lands in **FRD-13**. Navigable mockups: `prototype/party-proposal.html`, `prototype/party-pipeline.html`, embedded in place in `prototype/index.html` (auto-sizing iframes, no inner scroll). Full design spec: **`prototype/party-redesign-spec.md`**.
**Why:** FRD-06 misrepresented the engine вЂ” a generalist `implementer` per work order orchestrated by a deterministic script with document hand-offs (DR-013), NOT a team of specialists chatting live; the specialists live in *other phases*. The owner chose to fix the model before cementing the agent views. Faithfulness first, then the RPG magic. The owner validated the direction across the prototype iterations.

## 2026-06-17 вЂ” Resync of 3 FRD rollups + engine to v8.10.0 (derived FRD status)
**What:** Three FRDs вЂ” `frd-03-portfolio`, `frd-06-party`, `frd-08-documentation` вЂ” carried `implementation_status: PLANNED` in their `frd.md`/`blueprint.md` while **all their work orders were already `IN_REVIEW`** (built, awaiting their gate). The old engine only wrote the FRD rollup once everything was `VERIFIED`, so these documents misreported built features as "not started". Recomputed each FRD/blueprint rollup from its work orders (the source of truth) в†’ `IN_REVIEW`, and upgraded the engine to **v8.10.0**, which syncs rollups on plan + after each gate so this can't drift again. The work orders themselves were not touched.
**Why:** Surfaced while clarifying FRD-06's real state (it is **built and `IN_REVIEW`, awaiting the gate** вЂ” neither "verified" nor "not started"). Per the new source-of-truth rule (build-orchestration В§1 / DR-050), an FRD's status is derived from its work orders.
**Impact:** 6 docs (`frd.md` + `blueprint.md` of frd-03/06/08), `.claude/workflows/pandacorp-build.js`. Rule + engine: factory/plugin v8.10.0.

## 2026-06-17 вЂ” Build upgraded to v8.9.0 mid-stream (maxAgents brake + focused verify.sh --since)

## 2026-06-16 вЂ” WO-11-001 fix: deep-freeze BUILD_MODES catalog entries (B1 blocker from reviewer)
**What:** Fixed the shallow-freeze defect in `lib/constants.ts` (B1 from `docs/reviews/wo-11-001-review.md`). The original `Object.freeze([вЂ¦])` was shallow вЂ” the array itself was frozen but each entry object remained mutable, allowing `BUILD_MODES[0].id = "x"` to silently corrupt the catalog singleton for all consumers. Applied a deep-freeze: each entry is now wrapped with `Object.freeze(m)` inside a `.map()` before the outer `Object.freeze`. Added the reviewer-authored adversarial test suite `lib/build-modes.adversarial.test.ts` (20 tests, covering case/whitespace-variant modes, coercion-literal poison, JSON-object values, substring rejection, prototype-pollution keys, slug-with-`:` isolation, unicode slugs, and write-path throw-safety for `rememberMode`). All 61 WO-11-001 tests green; verify.sh (biome + tsc + vitest) passes.
**Why:** The reviewer (DR-015 different-model-family review) correctly identified that the immutability guarantee documented in the code comment was false at runtime. A mutation anywhere in the app would permanently corrupt the catalog singleton, breaking `getRememberedMode`'s `VALID_MODES` set and causing every validation check to pass unknown strings. Deep-freezing each entry is the correct fix: it causes `BUILD_MODES[0].id = "x"` to throw in strict mode (ESM files are always strict), making the corruption attempt visible and loud rather than silent.
**Impact:** Modified `mission-control/lib/constants.ts` (deep-freeze entries); added `mission-control/lib/build-modes.adversarial.test.ts`; `docs/api.md` updated (`BUILD_MODES is frozen` note now accurately says "deep-frozen").

## 2026-06-16 вЂ” WO-13-001: token schema validator + agent-color/state-vocab key maps (IF-13-tokens, IF-13-agent-colors, IF-13-state-vocab)
**What:** Implemented the pure TypeScript module `app/_design/tokens.ts` (WO-13-001). Exports: `validateTokenSchema` (validates `design-tokens.json` shape against blueprint В§3 contract вЂ” OKLCH keys, three theme variants including highContrast, all 10 agent roles, exactly 3 elevation levels, spacing scale, motion durations all <300ms, 2вЂ“3 easing tokens); `AGENT_ROLES` / `AgentRole` / `AGENT_COLOR` (canonical roleв†’CSS-token-key map, single source for FRD-06 and FRD-12 DAG); `AGENT_STATES` / `AgentState` / `STATE_BADGE` (icon+Spanish-label per state, 6 states вЂ” working/idle/failed/completed/blocked/reviewing). All 39 tests green; verify.sh (biome + tsc + vitest) passes. Published the internal module contract in `docs/api.md`.
**Why:** WO-13-001 establishes the typed contract that downstream UI WOs (FRD-06 Party, FRD-12 DAG, CMP-13-state-badge) depend on. Without it, every feature would define its own role/state vocabulary, creating duplication and drift. The `[key: string]: unknown` index signatures on `OklchTokens`, `ThemeTokens`, and `TokenSchema` are intentional вЂ” they allow the test file's `as Record<string, unknown>` cast pattern used for mutation testing (structuredClone + delete key). The `pick()` helper avoids biome's `useLiteralKeys` rule for dynamic key access on unknown records.
**Impact:** New `mission-control/app/_design/tokens.ts`, `mission-control/docs/api.md`; safe biome fixes applied to `app/_design/tokens.test.ts` and `components/CopyButton.test.tsx` (import ordering + format, no behavior change).

## 2026-06-16 вЂ” Pandacorp overlay materialized (6.0.0 в†’ 7.0.0): Mission Control becomes a buildable factory project
**What:** Mission Control was documented by hand inside the factory and never went through `/pandacorp:scaffold`, so it carried product docs + a hand-written `.pandacorp/status.yaml` but **none of the overlay machinery**. Materialized the full integration overlay from the v7 templates so `/pandacorp:blueprint` в†’ `/pandacorp:implement` can run on it: created `CLAUDE.md` + `AGENTS.md` (thin imports + durable conventions), `.pandacorp/guide.md` + `.pandacorp/README.md` (managed layer), `.claude/workflows/pandacorp-build.js` (the build engine вЂ” the previously missing blocker for `/implement`), `.claude/settings.json` (deny `rm -rf` / force-push / `.env` reads), a project-level `.gitignore` (adds `node_modules/.next/coverage/.env` on top of the root's MC ignores), and the gitignored `.pandacorp/comms/iteration.md`. Bumped `overlay_version` 6.0.0 в†’ 7.0.0 (`created_with` stays 6.0.0). The DR-049 feature-centric migration (upgrade step 2b) did NOT run вЂ” MC was already on that layout.
**Why:** The owner decided to build Mission Control with Pandacorp itself (dogfooding) instead of building it separately. An audit found MC's overlay was *declared* (status said 6.0.0) but never *materialized*; in particular the build engine `pandacorp-build.js` was absent, which would block `/implement`. This is the equivalent of a manual `/pandacorp:upgrade` for a never-scaffolded, in-factory project. MC is the special case of a project living INSIDE the factory repo, so its new `CLAUDE.md` records the deviations: no own git / never `git init`; factory root is one level up (`process.cwd()/..`, override `PANDACORP_FACTORY_ROOT`); `return_type` personal so the economic arc is skipped; `/release` = run locally on `127.0.0.1` (no deploy, no production gate).
**Impact:** New `mission-control/{CLAUDE.md, AGENTS.md, .gitignore}`, `mission-control/.claude/{settings.json, workflows/pandacorp-build.js}`, `mission-control/.pandacorp/{guide.md, README.md}`; `mission-control/.pandacorp/status.yaml` `overlay_version` в†’ 7.0.0. Pending before build: decide the v1 FRD scope (18 FRDs is too many for one blueprint), reconcile `PLAN.md` (its `git init` step doesn't apply in-repo; its state table predates the unified model), then `/pandacorp:blueprint`. Plugin-side follow-ups identified, not yet done: add the DR-045/048 preflight to the `blueprint` skill (it lacks the auto-upgrade that `implement`/`iterate`/`bug` have), and namespace `emit-event.sh` events by project so the Party panel can tell builds apart.

**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/prd.md` в†’ `docs/product/prd.md` (+ feature-landscape table); the 18 `docs/frds/frd-NN-<slug>.md` в†’ `docs/frds/frd-NN-<slug>/frd.md`; cross-reference fixes in `docs/product/prd.md`, `docs/design/brief.md`, `docs/decision-log.md` (header + two historical link targets) and the FRDs themselves; content updates to `frd-01-data-reading/frd.md`, `frd-05-work-orders/frd.md`, `frd-08-documentation/frd.md`; `mission-control/prototype/index.html` (doc-structure CONFIG/console surfaces, incl. DR-048 `.pandacorp/` drift fixed in passing). Factory side: standard `factory/standards/structure.md` (DR-049) + `factory/decisions/registry.yaml` + twin entry in `factory/decision-log.md`; live FRD-08 link target in root `CLAUDE.md` repointed. No Manual Reference change beyond the auto-derivation (DR-046).

## 2026-06-16 вЂ” FRD-18: Dashboard ("Inicio") as the landing command center
**What:** New **FRD-18**. Mission Control gains a **Dashboard** as its default landing view (the old behavior opened straight into a tab); the five tabs (Board/Portfolio/Achievements/Configuration/Manual) stay reachable from the nav. The dashboard is a read-only command center with five zones, top to bottom: (1) **Desde tu Гєltima visita** вЂ” a digest of *events* (work orders closed/failed, phase moves, decisions queued, lessons captured), not totals; (2) **Tu turno** вЂ” a queue of ONLY human-gate items (pending decisions, shipped-awaiting-`review-launch`, memory backlog nudge, ideas to prioritize) вЂ” `advance_pending` deliberately excluded (it lives on the Board); (3) **Pulso de la fГЎbrica** вЂ” a small funnel + the one metric that matters (ideaв†’shipped conversion) + the live/no-signal indicator; (4) **ConstrucciГіn y cartera** вЂ” per-project cards enriched with age-in-stage, *en vivo*/*sin seГ±al*, inline blocker reason, and shipped shown as *estable В· en operaciГіn*; (5) **Tu progreso** вЂ” the honest gamification strip (FRD-09). It composes FRD-09/12/13 and surfaces the FRD-01/15/16/17 banners. Built and approved iteratively in the prototype (`view: dashboard`): a first pass, then a research-informed v2 (added the digest, enriched the cartera, reframed the pulse as a funnel, dropped `advance_pending` from the queue per owner feedback).
**Why:** The owner asked for a landing screen that helps him *decide and take the next step* вЂ” "what needs me, where do I go" вЂ” with real value, not vanity metrics, plus a touch of honest gamification. We grounded the design in web research on analogous products (Devin Desktop's agent board, Linear Inbox, PagerDuty's "your open incidents", Vercel/GitHub-Actions build status, AgentCenter, Datadog's "alert on a lack of data", Kanban aging-WIP, HITL review-queue UX, NN/g action-centric dashboards, Lean Analytics OMTM, Octalysis White-Hat). The convergent principles: lead with a human-gate queue, manufacture substance from *events* (the since-last-visit digest) not counters, show age/stuck and no-signal not just status, tie every number to a decision, stay quiet when healthy, and reward outcomes only.
**The "Desde tu Гєltima visita" marker (key design call):** the owner flagged that with an always-open app, defining "last visit" as "last page load" would reset on every refresh and show nothing. Resolved: the `visto_hasta` marker is **persisted client-local state** (survives refresh and tab close) and advances ONLY on acknowledgement ("marcar visto") or on acting on an item вЂ” a refresh never moves it, so unseen events are never lost (email-style read/unread). When caught up, the section is never empty: it falls back to a dimmed last-24h rolling window, and (always-open) should tick up live as events arrive.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-18-dashboard.md` (new); `frd-01-data-reading.md` (reads the event stream for the digest + persists the local `visto_hasta` marker, clarified as UI state not a factory/project write); `docs/prd.md` (Scope v1 + product goal 0 + FRD range в†’ FRD-18); `mission-control/prototype/index.html` (new `dashboard` view + default landing, `digestSection()` with localStorage-backed seen marker, enriched portfolio cards, funnel pulse, `goproj`/`goidea`/`goboard`/`seen`/`seen-sim`/`seen-reset` handlers). Verified live in the preview: all zones render, navigation works, the seen-marker survives refresh, zero console errors. Spec-anchored mock data in the prototype; the Next.js app will read real events/state. Approved as a **first version** ("not 100% convinced, ship and iterate"). No Manual change needed вЂ” the dashboard is MC's own surface, not a new factory operable item (skills/agents/rules/standards), so DR-046's derived Reference is untouched.

## 2026-06-16 вЂ” Manual: "Autoaprendizaje" Concept page (self-learning, with diagram)
**What:** Added a new **Conceptos** page to Mission Control's Manual (the "CГіdice del gremio", FRD-08) explaining the self-learning loop in Spanish: an intro, a **flow diagram of the loop** (Capturar в†’ Refinar в†’ Cuaderno в†’ Recuperar, plus the gated Revisar в†’ TГє decides в†’ Promover branch + a "cada vuelta mГЎs lista" footer), the **3 actors** (cronista / `/memory` / `/learn`), the always-on general capture (3 tiers), the safety **protecciones** (A.U.D.N. dedup, provenance, candidateв†’active gate, human gate, the "more capture is not better" warning), the durable **promotions queue**, the lesson types, and where to see it. New `MANUALNAV` entry `c-autoaprendizaje` (doc:14) + a handler in `docPage()`; diagram built with the prototype's tokens/CSS (no new deps).
**Why:** The owner asked to document the self-learning system in the Manual with graphics so anyone can understand how it works. Closes the "add a Self-learning loop Concept page" item pending from the FRD-17 / DR-046 work.
**Impact:** `mission-control/prototype/index.html` (`MANUALNAV` + `docPage` handler). Verified in the live preview: the page renders, the diagram displays, navigation works, zero console errors. Hand-authored Concept page per DR-046's Guides/Concepts discipline (the Reference catalogs still auto-derive separately).

## 2026-06-16 вЂ” FRD-02: "Capture ideas" panel в†’ modal overlay
**What:** Changed the "Capture ideas / oportunidades" interaction from an inline collapsible panel (accordion) to a fixed modal overlay. The button stays always visible; clicking it opens a modal with dark backdrop + blur showing the four intake options (`explore`, `new-idea`, `discover`, `recommend`) as icon cards with description and copy-command row. Clicking the backdrop or вњ• closes it. Also corrected FRD-02: it was missing `/pandacorp:explore` from the intake command list.
**Why:** The accordion pushed the board content down and felt clunky. A modal keeps the board visible as context and makes the intake flow feel more deliberate. Owner's call.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board.md` (AC updated), `mission-control/prototype/index.html` (`intakePanel()` в†’ modal).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” FRD-03: missing-path badge + recovery command in Portfolio panel
**What:** Added acceptance criteria to **FRD-03** for the case where a project registered in the portfolio no longer exists on disk (folder deleted or moved): the Portfolio panel SHALL show a `вљ пёЏ path not found` badge on that project row, plus a copyable recovery command (`git clone <repo> <path>` + re-run sync-portfolio) if a `repo:` URL exists, or a plain warning if there is no remote. Same read-only + copyable-command pattern as FRD-15/16 banners. Badge disappears once the path is back on disk.
**Why:** The owner asked what happens when a project folder is deleted locally вЂ” the factory still tracks it but the user has no path forward. The plugin side (sync-portfolio step 4) now gives recovery instructions; the FRD side documents what the Next.js app must show when it reads the portfolio.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-03-portfolio.md` (new acceptance criteria). Plugin side: `plugin/skills/sync-portfolio/SKILL.md` + `plugin/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` (v6.1.1). Spec-only for MC вЂ” the prototype doesn't simulate it; the Next.js app will implement it when the Portfolio panel is built.

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” FRD-17: Proposals inbox (self-learning gate + self-suggestion)
**What:** New **FRD-17**. Mission Control gains a **Proposals inbox** ("Propuestas / CrГіnica del gremio") вЂ” the owner-facing surface of the self-learning loop (DR-047) and the place where MC suggests improvements on its own. It aggregates four streams: candidate lessons from `factory/memory/`, promotion proposals (a recurring lesson в†’ standard/rule/skill), prune proposals from `/pandacorp:memory review`, and **self-suggestions** MC computes locally (bottlenecks, velocity alerts, unused skill/agent, decision-rule friction, a lesson recurring across в‰Ґ2 projects, a shipped project that merits `/pandacorp:review-launch`). For each, it shows the evidence + the exact command to act вЂ” and never acts itself (read-only, like FRD-15/16). Extends FRD-14's chips with a proposals stream; honest/dismissible per FRD-09. Also a **memory-health panel** (owner's request): pending raw-note count, candidate-lesson count, and `/pandacorp:memory` last-run staleness, with a nudge command when there's a backlog вЂ” it doubles as the on-demand refine trigger, so the cadence is scheduled sweep + this reminder (NOT tied to `implement`). And a durable **promotions queue** (lessons carry a `promotion: proposed/approved/rejected` field set by `/memory review` + `learn`): the owner reviews the full list of rules-to-promote and decides whenever вЂ” via `/pandacorp:memory status` today and this page when the app is built (owner's request).
**Why:** The owner asked for two things on Mission Control: a place to approve the lessons/promotions the factory learns, and for the app to "auto-suggest" improvements the more it is used, without being asked вЂ” the human gate of DR-047 and the visible face of the loop (`docs/proposals/09-self-learning-factory.md`). Computing suggestions locally from data MC already reads (events, status, portfolio, `factory/memory/`) keeps it read-only and Claude-call-free (FRD-01).
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-17-proposals-inbox.md` (new). Spec-only вЂ” Mission Control isn't built yet (the prototype will simulate it). Factory side: the loop's engine shipped in plugin v6.1.0 (`librarian` agent + `/pandacorp:memory`), DR-047. Pending: reconcile the prototype Manual catalogs (the new `memory` skill, `librarian` agent, DR-047/DR-048) and add a "Self-learning loop" Concept page (DR-046, FRD-08).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Read the new .pandacorp/ project layer; MC dogfoods it (DR-048)
**What:** Project state moved from `docs/status.yaml` to `.pandacorp/status.yaml` (DR-048), so the data-reading FRDs were updated: FRD-01/02/04/14/16 now read `.pandacorp/status.yaml` and the `.pandacorp/inbox/` (bugs, decisions) + `.pandacorp/comms/` layers. Mission Control **dogfoods** the new structure: its own `docs/{status.yaml,idea-origin.md,summary.md}` moved to `mission-control/.pandacorp/`.
**Why:** Consistency with the factory's new project structure (see `factory/decision-log.md`, same date, DR-048). MC reads every project's state; that path changed.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/{frd-01,frd-02,frd-04,frd-14,frd-16}.md` (paths), `mission-control/.pandacorp/{status.yaml,idea-origin.md,comms/summary.md}` (moved), root `.gitignore` (MC comms paths). The HTML prototype's mock paths are cosmetic; reconcile when the Next.js app reads real files.

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Manual (FRD-08) reflects the factory: derived Reference + reconciled prototype (DR-046)
**What:** FRD-08 now requires the Manual's **Reference** catalogs (commands, agents, decision rules, standards) to be **derived from the canonical source** at build/read time вЂ” the plugin skill+agent frontmatter under `plugin/skills/` & `plugin/agents/`, `factory/decisions/registry.yaml`, `factory/standards/` вЂ” not a hand-maintained copy, plus a criterion that the Manual stays in sync (Reference auto-derived; Guides/Concepts by the documentation discipline). Reconciled the HTML prototype's catalogs against today's factory: added skills `review-launch` + `adopt`, agent `implementer`, rules DR-040..DR-046, and the `documentation` standard вЂ” closing a drift of 2 skills / 1 agent / 6 rules / 1 standard. Catalog now: 20 skills (7 fГЎbrica + 13 proyecto), 13 agents, 46 rules (last DR-046), 14 standards.
**Why:** Owner's rule (DR-046, see [factory/decision-log.md](../../factory/decision-log.md) same date): every relevant factory-workflow change must surface in the Manual, and the future Next.js app must build the Reference from the real artifacts so it can't drift. The prototype had fallen behind вЂ” exactly the failure the rule prevents.
**Context:** Mechanism chosen by the owner = derive the Reference (drift-proof) + discipline for the hand-authored prose. The prototype's `CONFIG.{skills,agents,rules,estandares}` arrays remain the hand-reconciled stand-in until the Next.js app derives the catalogs from source (FRD-08 prototype note).
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-08-documentation.md`, `mission-control/prototype/index.html` (`CONFIG` arrays). Factory-side: `factory/decisions/registry.yaml` (DR-046) + root `CLAUDE.md` ("Decision log" section) вЂ” twin entry in `factory/decision-log.md` (same date). Verified in preview: Referencia в†’ Comandos renders the reconciled catalog (the new `/review-launch` and `/adopt` cards appear; counts 7+13), no console errors; CONFIG counts confirmed by evaluation (20/13/46/14).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” FRD-16: orphan-project detection (adopt? banner)
**What:** New FRD-16. Mission Control scans the projects folder (`projects_path` from the profile, else the factory's parent) for git repos that are NOT in the portfolio and have NO Pandacorp marker, and surfaces them as a dismissible "Unregistered project вЂ” adopt?" banner pointing to `/pandacorp:adopt`. A folder WITH the marker but missing from the portfolio suggests `/pandacorp:sync-portfolio` instead. Read-only and bounded to the projects folder's immediate children; sibling of FRD-15 (plugin drift): detect a gap, show the command, don't act.
**Why:** The new brownfield path (DR-045, `/pandacorp:adopt`) needs a way to be discovered вЂ” otherwise an external project the owner built stays invisible to the factory. This closes the loop so Mission Control nudges adoption, mirroring how FRD-15 nudges the plugin update.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-16-orphan-project-detection.md` (new). Factory side: `factory/decisions/registry.yaml` (DR-045), `factory/decision-log.md` (same date). Spec-only вЂ” Mission Control isn't built yet (the prototype simulates it with an `ORPHANS` flag).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Board column derivation (phase bridge), portfolio business columns, drift-banner fix
**What:** FRD-02 now **derives** a card's column from two axes (card status pre-project; the project's `phase` for `in-pipeline` cards) instead of grouping by `status` alone вЂ” fixing the design/architecture/building columns that no card status ever produced (mapping: productв†’Documentada, designв†’DiseГ±o, architectureв†’Arquitectura, implementation/releaseв†’building, operationв†’shipped; missing project в†’ falls back to Documentada). FRD-01 reads the project phase as the column source for in-pipeline cards and also reads `pending_bugs`/`last_green_sha`/`safe_to_test`. FRD-03 shows each shipped project's business snapshot (users/return/verdict from `/pandacorp:review-launch`, DR-043). FRD-15's drift banner now compares `gitCommitSha` (not the semver `version`, which never matched). Mission Control's own `status.yaml` got the 5 missing template fields.
**Why:** The re-audit found the board couldn't place mid-pipeline cards from the frontmatter alone (the card freezes at `in-pipeline`), and the drift banner read the wrong field so it couldn't warn when the installed plugin fell behind.
**Context:** The prototype (mock data) still groups by a `status` that crams the column value in; the real Next.js app implements the FRD-02 derivation вЂ” not worth rewriting the 2.4 MB mock now.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/{frd-01,frd-02,frd-03,frd-15}.md`, `mission-control/docs/status.yaml`. Factory-side state model: `factory/decision-log.md` and `factory/ideas/decision-log.md` (same date).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Mission Control's UI is in Spanish (made explicit)

The underlying code/identifiers stay English; only the UI copy is Spanish. This is the committed exception to "committed = English".

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Title "Pandacorp Mission Control" + Guild vs Party codified
**What:** (1) The app's visible title becomes **"Pandacorp Mission Control"** (topbar + `<title>`): Pandacorp (brand) + Mission Control (the app). (2) It was clarified that **Guild (gremio)** and **Party** are two **distinct** RPG layers вЂ” not synonyms вЂ” and the boundary was **codified** in [FRD-09](frds/frd-09-gamification/frd.md): guild = the operator/factory meta layer (level/XP, guild Hall/Codex/Commands); party = the agents of one concrete project (RPG panel, FRD-06). The phrases where they were mixed were cleaned up ("The party works in the guildвЂ¦" в†’ "вЂ¦in its roomвЂ¦"; PARTY.md "by a guild" в†’ "by the guild's room").
**Why:** The owner noticed "guild" in several places and wondered if it was the same as Party. It isn't (a guild has many parties); both layers are intentional. Writing down the boundary avoids confusing them in the future.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-09-gamification.md` (new "Vocabulary: Guild vs Party" section), `mission-control/PARTY.md`, `mission-control/prototype/index.html` (title + feed).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Rename: the app is "Mission Control"; the RPG panel is "Party"
**What:** We reassigned the names. The **whole app** (formerly "cockpit") is now called **Mission Control** вЂ” the center from which the entire factory is controlled. The **per-project RPG panel** (formerly "Mission Control") becomes **Party**: the subtab where you see your party of agents working live. "Pandacorp" remains the factory/brand. The `cockpit/` в†’ `mission-control/` folder was renamed, the panel's canonical docs (`MISSION-CONTROL.md` в†’ `PARTY.md`, `frd-06-mission-control.md` в†’ `frd-06-party.md`), the prototype (topbar, `<title>`, "Party" subtab, manual texts) and `.claude/launch.json`. Verified in preview: "Mission Control" topbar, "Party" subtab, RPG map and KPIs intact, no console errors.
**Why:** By convention (NASA, macOS), "Mission Control" names the center that supervises and commands the ENTIRE operation, not a sub-panel; having it on the little panel inverted the meaning and was sometimes used as a synonym for the app. The analogy now is clean: Pandacorp (organization) в†’ Mission Control (its control center = the app) в†’ Party (the crew of agents on each mission, in line with the "party" language the prototype already used).
**Impact:** the `mission-control/` folder (formerly `cockpit/`), `mission-control/PARTY.md`, `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-06-party.md`, `mission-control/prototype/index.html`, `.claude/launch.json`. Repo-wide change (CLAUDE.md, README, plugin/skills, standards, registry.yaml, hook): see the twin entry in [factory/decision-log.md](../../factory/decision-log.md).

## 2026-06-15 вЂ” Onboarding gate + board tags (category + return)
**What:** Mission Control gains an **onboarding gate**: if it doesn't find `factory/profile.md`, it shows вЂ” before anything else вЂ” a banner asking to run `/pandacorp:onboarding` (FRD-01). On the board, each card goes from a single tag (monetizable/personal/both) to **two**: **category** (solution type: web/mobile/desktop/AI/claude-code/prompts/automation/CLI/rework) with an icon, and **return** (monetary/opportunity/personal/mixed) with color; the filter is now by category (FRD-02). HTML prototype updated and verified in preview.
**Why:** Without a profile the factory can't make aligned recommendations (hence the gate). A single binary tag captured neither the project type nor the return model (money or opportunity); two orthogonal axes make it clear on the board.
**Impact:** `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-01-data-reading.md`, `mission-control/docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board.md`, `mission-control/prototype/index.html`. Related: `factory/ideas/_idea-template.md`, DR-039.

## 2026-06-14 вЂ” Mission Control decision log created
**What:** The Mission Control decision log starts.
**Why:** Part of the factory's "document everything" discipline вЂ” see [factory/decision-log.md](../../factory/decision-log.md).
